# 🌶️ Pepper DS ii Core: Bell - Foundations — DesignBridge

> **AI AGENT INSTRUCTIONS — READ FIRST, APPLY TO ALL OUTPUT**
>
> This file is the complete visual specification for **"🌶️ Pepper DS ii Core: Bell - Foundations — DesignBridge"**.
> The YAML front matter above contains the normative design tokens. The sections below explain how to apply them.
> Apply every rule to every line of UI, HTML, CSS, JSX, or component code you generate.
>
> 1. **Colours** — Use only exact hex values or `var(--token)` names from this file. No substitutions.
> 2. **Typography** — Match font family, weight, size, line-height exactly.
> 3. **Spacing** — Use only values from the spacing/sizing token tables.
> 4. **Border radius** — Use only the defined radius tokens.
> 5. **Components** — Mirror defined structures. Honour variant property names exactly.
> 6. **Shadows** — Apply defined elevation styles. Do not invent shadows.
> 7. **Themes** — Use the `themes` block for dark mode / multi-theme support. Apply correct mode tokens.
> 8. **Unknowns** — If a visual decision is not defined here, ask before inventing it.

## Shadows & Effects

> Apply these exact values. Do not invent new shadows.

### icon light effect

```css
box-shadow: inset 0px -3px 2px #347ffc1a, inset 2px 3px 2px #ffffff1a;
```
- `backdrop-filter: blur(15px);`

### icon dark effect

```css
box-shadow: 0px 4px 6px -1px #0a0a0a0d, inset -3px 3px 14px #ffffff4d, inset 15px -15px 27px #00000033, inset 0px -1px 2px #00276833;
```

### focus/default

```css
box-shadow: 0px 0px 0px 4px #0064fa, 0px 0px 0px 2px #ffffff;
```

### focus/error

```css
box-shadow: 0px 0px 0px 4px #e7000b, 0px 0px 0px 2px #ffffff;
```

### focus/subtle

```css
box-shadow: 0px 0px 0px 4px #0a0a0a, 0px 0px 0px 2px #ffffff;
```

### focus/inverse/subtle

```css
box-shadow: 0px 0px 0px 4px #ffffff, 0px 0px 0px 2px #0a0a0a;
```

### shadow/shadow_2xs

- `box-shadow: 0px 1px 1px 0px #0a0a0a0d;`

### shadow/shadow_xs

- `box-shadow: 0px 1px 2px 0px #0a0a0a0d;`

### shadow/shadow_sm

- `box-shadow: 0px 2px 4px -1px #0a0a0a0d;`

### shadow/shadow_md

- `box-shadow: 0px 4px 6px -1px #0a0a0a1a;`

### shadow/shadow_lg

- `box-shadow: 0px 10px 14px -4px #0a0a0a1a;`

### shadow/shadow_xl

- `box-shadow: 0px 20px 24px -6px #0a0a0a1a;`

### shadow/shadow_2xl

- `box-shadow: 0px 24px 48px -12px #0a0a0a40;`

### blur/xs

- `backdrop-filter: blur(4px);`
- `backdrop-filter: blur(4px);`

### blur/sm

- `backdrop-filter: blur(8px);`
- `backdrop-filter: blur(8px);`

### blur/md

- `backdrop-filter: blur(12px);`
- `backdrop-filter: blur(12px);`

### blur/lg

- `backdrop-filter: blur(16px);`
- `backdrop-filter: blur(16px);`

### blur/xl

- `backdrop-filter: blur(40px);`
- `backdrop-filter: blur(40px);`

### blur/2xl

- `backdrop-filter: blur(40px);`
- `backdrop-filter: blur(40px);`

### blur/3xl

- `backdrop-filter: blur(64px);`
- `backdrop-filter: blur(64px);`

## Design Rules — Mandatory for AI Agents

| Category | Rule |
|----------|------|
| Colours | Use only tokens defined above. Always output as `var(--token)`. Never hard-code. |
| Typography | Match family, weight, size, line-height exactly from the table above. |
| Spacing | Use only spacing token values. No arbitrary numbers. |
| Radius | Use only border-radius tokens. No arbitrary values. |
| Shadows | Use only defined elevation/effect styles. |
| Components | Replicate structures. Honour variant property names. |
| Themes | Implement all defined themes. Use CSS custom properties with mode-specific overrides. |
| HTML | Output semantic HTML5 with ARIA roles. All components responsive by default. |
| Unknowns | If a decision is not defined here: ask the user, do not invent. |

### Theme Overrides

```css
/* Theme: Tablet (source: Responsive ) */
[data-theme="tablet"] {
  --canvas-viewport-width: 768px;
  --canvas-viewport-height: 1024px;
  --canvas-canvas-columns: 8px;
  --theme-spacing-layout-gutter: 20px;
  --theme-spacing-layout-margin: 40px;
  --theme-spacing-layout-pad: 64px;
  --theme-spacing-layout-gap-lg: 40px;
  --theme-spacing-content-pad-sm: 24px;
  --theme-spacing-layout-gap-md: 24px;
  --theme-spacing-content-pad-md: 32px;
  --theme-spacing-content-gap-md: 24px;
  --theme-spacing-content-pad-lg: 40px;
  --theme-spacing-content-gap-lg: 40px;
  --theme-spacing-content-gap-xs: 16px;
  --theme-spacing-layout-gutter-stack-md: 20px;
  --theme-spacing-layout-gutter-stack-lg: 32px;
  --theme-spacing-layout-gutter-stack-sm: 20px;
  --theme-spacing-content-gap-sm: 24px;
}
```
